<rating>4< /rating><user_id>105330578909981949868< /user_id>< Time>
1456444843224</Time>
<Text>Though this is gentrified-gabacho-Latin-fusion-foodfare, this pocha really likes this place! I mean, I'm here like every week! This used to be Burrito King (RIP) and though I was sad to see that place go, I love Mixto's burritos and tacos made with organic humane meats like chicken, pork and beef. Plus, with all the lovely fixins, customers can select a salsa to be added to their meal. Very fresh! Dee-lishhhhh!!! Plus, it's organic!

Besides their tacos and burritos, they also have bowls, which is not something we Latinos are accustomed to. But, we like it anyway. ;) Still great flavors with cilantro, onions, salsa, queso y todo! That's right, vatos locos!

Another special item that can be found here are their fried plantains, also known as maduros in the Cuban world, cooked to perfection, along with a dollop of crema mexicana! So delicate and delicious! I could seriously eat these all the time! (Why does it seem like I'm yelling while  writing this review?)

In addition to the things mentioned above, they have specials like almond horchata. If you haven't tried it yet, you must! It's delicately sweet with a touch of cinnamon and a lovely texture. It's delightful, really.

Plus, they sometimes have great desserts like their key lime pie. Once again, delicately sweet.

In addition to their great food, these folks are doing their part in being eco-friendly, like having different portals for recycling and composting. And if you know me, this brings a smile to this earth-loving gal!

And, the people that work here are awesome! They are so refreshingly nice. So chill and willing to engage in conversation. :)

The prices for the food here are decently priced, especially for what you get! (Burrito King prices?)

The only problem about Mixto is the location. Why? It's located in one of the busiest sections of Silver Lake--right across from the insane Trader Joe's parking lot and near the intersection of Hyperion and Rowena. (If you have driven around this area, you know exactly what I'm talking about!!!). Plus, they have a somewhat smallish parking lot, though I never encountered issues with finding a spot. But, other than this, Mixto is great!

Oh! I forgot to mention that they have a handicapped parking space where a person with a disability can order their meal without ever having to leaving their vehicle. (It's like one of those ordering things found at a drive-thru). So convenient. :)

I love this place!</Text><Pics>None<//Pics><gmapID>0x80c2c0c917ccba59:0x9f94867f22e6b064< /gmapID>< Resp>

< text>
I've coming here for 30 years, growing up in Rancho this place has been a staple for all sports organizations for years as you can see by the many, many team plaques on the walls from over 40 years worth of memories for all involved.

It's always quick friendly service, from the moment you walk in and order, until you're finishing up they check on you to make sure you have everything you need and take away anything you don't.

I've honestly never had a bad experience here, it's great to see that even through ownership change they've kept the family feel my family has come to know and love over the years, all while keeping up to date and growing with the times.

Now I get to bring my son here to celebrate together with the family the same way I did growing up and that's the best thing about this place, 4 generations in and this is still our favorite place to get together.<//text>

4</rate>
< text>
tl;dr:
-Great local noodle shop: lots of options (stir fried). Noodle soup options limited.
-Friendly service: they go above and beyond!

PARKING: Shared private lot or street

FOOD:
Taiwanese beef noodle soup: I've definitely had my fair share of beef noodle soup, and I do like Honey Badger's broth more than others. They give a heaping portion of beef, but their noodles themselves leave a bit of longing for a slightly thinner noodle.
Fontina cheese noodles: I've always told my boyfriend that noodles and pasta are not so different, and this dish proves it. Think of a great mac and cheese made with chewy noodles - definitely a hit. Make sure you add bacon to amp up the flavor!

SERVICE: Very friendly. Our server was very interactive and made sure to suggest some options that he thought we would enjoy. They also offered samples of new test drinks which I thought was a nice touch. Stellar focus on customer service.

TIP:
-Great place if you like customization. You can build your own stir fry noodle plate!</text>

< review>
I had a great experience here on the 4th of July when I came in with a really irritated and red eye.

Because it's a Cedars Sinai location, I was worried a visit here was considered a trip to the emergency room and would be very expensive. Instead, my health insurance provider recommended this location for urgent care. My insurance told me to first call to re-confirm they took my insurance. They did. They take all PPO insurance.

The wait was 10 minutes. The clinician,  Mr. Turnipseed, asked lots of questions about my eye and had a look at it with a fluorescent light. He prescribed an eyedrop for allergies. It is literally 2 hours later and it feels 95% fixed.

The quality of care I received was better than most non-urgent care physicians I visit. This was for a chronic condition, so lot of doctors have tried lots of things over the years. This clinician listened to me and found a solution that everyone else missed. TRY THIS PLACE!< /review>

I have received no phone calls and now it's after 4pm on Christmas eve and I still have no couch. They are closed so I'm assuming I will not have a couch tomorrow.
